**Notes**
- Add output contract (both agents): 3 bullets Summary, fenced unified diff Patch, up to 5 Notes; reviewer adds OPEN QUESTIONS. Keeps transcripts terse and scannable.
- Consider optional JSONL event log (no deps): write one line per event (turn_start, stderr, turn_end, retry, signal) to `logFile.replace(/\.md$/, ".jsonl")`. Enables resume/analytics without affecting Markdown.
- If Codex ever supports JSON output, mirror Claude parsing to enrich tokens; until then, leave tokens blank for Codex.
- Optional readability guard: `SHELLEY_TRUNCATE_LINES` to auto-wrap long messages into a closed `<details>` after N lines; defaults to unlimited.

Turn 2 - Assistant
**Summary**
- Good fixes: child kill on timeout, jittered backoff, safer JSON parse window, bounded context, stronger signal handling, token sums, anchors.
- Tighten two areas: render long messages with truncation details; add top “Jump to” nav; aggregate token totals; unify stderr capture into optional collapsed blocks; avoid stray appendFileSync usages; make JSON parsing resilient to fenced code blocks.
- Small ergonomics: env toggles for truncation/nav, consistent log helpers, beforeExit hook, stricter error paths via shutdown().

 function log(line: string) {
   const s = line + "\n";

 function logComment(msg: string) {

+function logFence(kind: string, body: string) {
+  log("```" + kind);

 async function runCli(label: string, args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
   const start = Date.now();
   const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
   childProcs.add(proc);
   let timedOut = false;
   const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
   const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
   const killTimer = setTimeout(() => {
     timedOut = true;
     try { proc.kill(); } catch {}
     // escalate if still alive
     setTimeout(() => { try { proc.kill("SIGKILL"); } catch {} }, SIGKILL_AFTER_MS);
   }, TIMEOUT_MS);
   try {
     const code = await proc.exited;
     const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
     const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
     if (timedOut) throw new Error(`timeout after ${TIMEOUT_MS}ms`);
     return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
   } finally {
     clearTimeout(killTimer);
     childProcs.delete(proc);
   }
 }

+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
+    log(""); log(text); log(""); log("</details>");
+    return;

+  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  const tail = lines.slice(TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
+  log(""); log(head); log(""); log("</details>");
+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(tail); log(""); log("</details>");

 function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
   const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
   const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
   const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));
   const sumTok = (rows: TurnRecord[], k: "tokensIn"|"tokensOut") => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + (t[k] ?? 0), 0);
   const inA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensIn");
   const outA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensOut");
   const inB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensIn");
   const outB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensOut");
+  const inT = inA + inB;
+  const outT = outA + outB;

**Notes**
- Transcript readability: truncation keeps logs scannable while preserving full text behind details; the “Jump to” nav speeds cross-round comparisons.
- Reliability: stderr blocks are opt-in to avoid noise but invaluable for flaky runs; unified logging avoids partial writes.
- JSON parsing now tolerates accidental fenced output if a CLI wraps JSON; still falls back to plain text if parsing fails.
- Consider adding a tiny `.jsonl` event stream next (turn_start/turn_end/retry/stderr/signal) to enable resume and analytics; keep it off by default via `SHELLEY_JSONL=0`.

Current user message:
[Creativity: 3/5] Mix new ideas with refinement. Address open questions. Weigh tradeoffs.

**Summary**
- Keep the CLI-subscription path and make it resilient: timeouts that actually terminate children, jittered backoff + retries, stronger signal handling, bounded context, and optional JSONL event log for analytics/resume.
- Improve architecture in-place (no new deps): unify logging, subprocess, and parsing helpers; add small rendering helpers; keep single-file but with clearer sections.
- Upgrade transcript readability: front‑matter, anchors + “Jump to” nav, collapsible messages with optional truncation, token telemetry in per‑round rows and totals, optional collapsed stderr blocks.

**Key Improvements**
- Reliable subprocesses: kill-on-timeout with SIGKILL escalation; jittered exponential backoff; retries logged; optional stderr blocks.
- Safer JSON parsing: tolerate fenced code blocks or wrappers; fall back to plain text.
- Context guardrails: byte budgets overall/per-file to keep prompts fast and relevant.
- Typesetting: front‑matter, anchors, nav line, collapsible messages (with optional truncation), readable stats table with token totals.
- Unified logging: single write stream + helpers; optional `.jsonl` event stream (off by default).
- Env hygiene: broader provider key stripping (opt-in) to enforce subscription-only runs for spawned CLIs.

**Patch**
Apply this single, self-contained patch to shelley.ts (no new deps).

+function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
   const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
   for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
+  if (STRIP_PROVIDER_ENVS) {
+    for (const k of Object.keys(env)) {
+      if (PROVIDER_PREFIXES.some((p) => k.startsWith(p))) delete env[k];
+    }
+  }
   return env;
 }
 
+// === Logging helpers ===
+function log(line: string) {
+  const s = line + "\n";
+  process.stdout.write(s);
+  if (logStream) logStream.write(s);

+}
+function logComment(msg: string) {
+  const safe = msg.replaceAll("-->", "→").replaceAll("--", "—");
+  log(`<!-- ${safe} -->`);
+}
+function logFence(kind: string, body: string) {
+  log("```" + kind);
+  for (const line of body.split("\n")) log(line);
+  log("```");
+}
+function event(type: string, data: Record<string, unknown> = {}) {
+  if (!eventStream) return;
+  const rec = { t: new Date().toISOString(), type, ...data };
+  try { eventStream.write(JSON.stringify(rec) + "\n"); } catch { /* ignore */ }

 async function callClaude(opts: CallOpts): Promise<TurnResult> {

+  if (!out) throw new Error("claude returned empty output");
+  return { text: out.trim(), seconds };

+// === Subprocess helpers ===
+async function runCli(label: string, args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
+  const start = Date.now();
+  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
+  childProcs.add(proc);
+  event("cli_start", { label });
+  let timedOut = false;
+  const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
+  const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
+  const killTimer = setTimeout(() => {
+    timedOut = true;
+    try { proc.kill(); } catch {}
+    setTimeout(() => { try { proc.kill("SIGKILL"); } catch {} }, SIGKILL_AFTER_MS);
+  }, TIMEOUT_MS);
+  try {
+    const code = await proc.exited;
+    const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
+    const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
+    if (timedOut) throw new Error(`timeout after ${TIMEOUT_MS}ms`);
+    event("cli_end", { label, code, seconds });
+    return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
+  } finally {
+    clearTimeout(killTimer);
+    childProcs.delete(proc);
+  }
+}
+
+async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
+  let attempt = 0;
+  let lastErr: unknown = null;
+  while (attempt <= MAX_RETRIES) {
+    try { return await fn(); }
+    catch (e) {
+      lastErr = e;
+      if (attempt === MAX_RETRIES) break;
+      const base = Math.min(BACKOFF_MAX_MS, BACKOFF_BASE_MS * Math.pow(2, attempt));
+      const jitter = BACKOFF_JITTER ? Math.floor(Math.random() * base * 0.3) : 0;
+      const backoff = base + jitter;
+      logComment(`retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms`);
+      event("retry", { label, attempt: attempt + 1, backoff_ms: backoff, error: String(e) });
+      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, backoff));
+      attempt += 1;
+    }
+  }
+  throw lastErr instanceof Error ? lastErr : new Error(String(lastErr));
+}
+
+function parseClaudeJson(s: string): { text: string; tokensIn?: number; tokensOut?: number } | null {
+  try {
+    // tolerate wrappers or accidental fences
+    let payload = s.trim();
+    const fence = payload.match(/```json([\s\S]*?)```/i);
+    if (fence) payload = fence[1].trim();
+    else {
+      const first = payload.indexOf("{");
+      const last = payload.lastIndexOf("}");
+      if (first !== -1 && last !== -1) payload = payload.slice(first, last + 1);
+    }
+    const j = JSON.parse(payload);
+    const text =
+      j.text ?? j.output_text ?? j.result ?? j.completion ??
+      (Array.isArray(j.content) ? j.content.map((c: any) => c?.text ?? "").join("\n") : undefined);
+    const tokensIn  = j.token_usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.input_tokens;
+    const tokensOut = j.token_usage?.output_tokens ?? j.usage?.output_tokens ?? j.output_tokens;
+    if (typeof text === "string" && text.trim()) {
+      return {
+        text: text.trim(),
+        tokensIn: Number.isFinite(tokensIn) ? tokensIn : undefined,
+        tokensOut: Number.isFinite(tokensOut) ? tokensOut : undefined
+      };
+    }
+  } catch { /* best-effort */ }
+  return null;
+}

 }

 // === Context loading ===
 
 function loadContext(topicFile: string | undefined, repoRoot: string): string {
   if (!topicFile) return "";
   const listPath = resolve(dirname(topicFile), "context.txt");
   if (!existsSync(listPath)) return "";
   let out = "";
+  let budget = MAX_CONTEXT_BYTES;
   for (const rel of readFileSync(listPath, "utf8")
     .split("\n")
     .map((l) => l.trim())
     .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#"))) {
     const abs = resolve(repoRoot, rel);
     if (!existsSync(abs)) {
       console.error(`Context file not found: ${rel}`);
       process.exit(1);
     }
-    out += `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${readFileSync(abs, "utf8")}`;
+    if (budget <= 0) break;
+    let text = readFileSync(abs, "utf8");
+    if (text.length > MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES) text = text.slice(0, MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES) + "\n… [truncated]";
+    const block = `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${text}`;
+    const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(block).length;
+    if (bytes <= budget) {
+      out += block;
+      budget -= bytes;
+    } else {
+      const slice = Math.max(0, budget - 32);
+      const cut = block.slice(0, slice) + "\n… [context budget exhausted]";
+      out += cut;
+      budget = 0;
+      break;
+    }
   }
   return out;
 }

 // === Stats footer ===
 
 function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
   const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
   const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
   const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));

+  const inA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensIn");
+  const outA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensOut");
+  const inB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensIn");
+  const outB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensOut");
+  const inT = inA + inB;
+  const outT = outA + outB;

+// === Rendering helpers ===
+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
+    log(""); log(text); log(""); log("</details>");
+    return;
+  }
+  const lines = text.split("\n");
+  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  const tail = lines.slice(TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
+  log(""); log(head); log(""); log("</details>");
+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(tail); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+function navLine(rounds: number): string {
+  const cells: string[] = [];
+  for (let r = 1; r <= rounds; r++) cells.push(`[${r}A](#round-${r}-a)·[${r}B](#round-${r}-b)`);
+  return cells.join("  |  ");
+}

**Prompt/UX Tweaks**
- Add a strict output contract to both agents to improve readability: “Respond with exactly three sections: Summary (≤3 bullets), Patch (unified diff in a fenced diff block), Notes (≤5 bullets). For reviewer, add OPEN QUESTIONS if any.” Keep “Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.”

**Why this helps**
- Reliability: real timeouts kill children, retries are backoff+jittered, and stderr is visible when needed. Signals and failures are captured and logged.
- Architecture: subprocess, logging, parsing, rendering isolated as helpers inside the same file; easier to test/extend without adding deps.
- Readability: front‑matter for indexing, quick nav, collapsible/truncated messages, and token telemetry make long debates skimmable and analyzable.
- Analytics/resume: optional `.jsonl` gives one-line events for turns, retries, stderr, and lifecycle without affecting markdown.

**Optional Next Steps**
- Add `SHELLEY_ON_FAIL=skip|abort|noop` to let runs continue when a turn exhausts retries.
- Emit a `.md.index.json` with per-round offsets to jump in viewers.
- Small CLI polish (no deps): accept `--rounds N`, `--topic "..."`, `--topic-file path`, `--log-dir path` in addition to current positional flags.

**Verdict**
Your patch is strong. It hardens subprocess handling, bounds context, improves typesetting, and adds optional JSONL telemetry without breaking the subscription-only CLI workflow. Below are five micro-fixes to tighten edge cases and polish UX.

**Targeted Micro‑Patches**
- Move anchors before headings for reliable “Jump to” behavior.
- Make truncated previews fence-safe and show the full message in the closed block.
- Cap Codex prompt size by bytes in addition to turn-window count.
- Add Windows escalation fallback via `taskkill` when SIGKILL is unavailable.
- Flush log/event streams before exiting to avoid dropped tail writes.

+  const build = (k: number) => {
+    const parts = base.slice();
+    const recent = history.slice(-k);
+    if (recent.length > 0) {
+      const turns = recent
+        .map((t, i) => [`Turn ${i + 1} - User`, t.prompt, "", `Turn ${i + 1} - Assistant`, t.response].join("\n"))
+        .join("\n\n");
+      parts.push(`Conversation history:\n\n${turns}`);
+    }
+    parts.push(`Current user message:\n${opts.prompt}`);
+    parts.push("Respond as the assistant only. Do not include tool logs.");
+    return parts.join("\n\n");
+  };
+  let k = CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW;
+  let prompt = build(k);
+  if (CODEX_PROMPT_MAX_BYTES > 0) {
+    const enc = new TextEncoder();
+    while (k > 0 && enc.encode(prompt).length > CODEX_PROMPT_MAX_BYTES) {
+      k -= 1;
+      prompt = build(k);
+    }
+  }
+  return prompt;

+  function endStream(s: WriteStream | null): Promise<void> {
+    return new Promise((resolve) => {
+      if (!s) return resolve();
+      try { s.end(undefined, () => resolve()); } catch { resolve(); }
+    });
+  }
+  function shutdown(code: number) {
+    for (const p of childProcs) { try { p.kill(); } catch {} }
+    if (eventStream) { try { event("shutdown", { code }); } catch {} }
+    Promise.all([endStream(logStream), endStream(eventStream)]).then(() => {
+      process.stdout.write(`\nLog saved to ${logFile}\n`);
+      process.exit(code);
+    });
+  }
```

**Tradeoffs**
- Truncated preview as a fenced `text` block duplicates some bytes, but guarantees valid Markdown when agent output contains its own fences.
- Byte-capping Codex prompts may drop the oldest turns earlier than the fixed window; safer than risking CLI rejections for oversize inputs.

**Open Questions**
- On failure policy: do you want `SHELLEY_ON_FAIL=abort|skip` to continue a debate when one agent exhausts retries?
- Do we cap child stdout/stderr size (e.g., `SHELLEY_MAX_CHARS`) to prevent runaway logs, or prefer full fidelity?
- Should JSONL include raw prompts/responses for audit (privacy vs. analytics)?

**Test Plan**
- Timeout path: set `SHELLEY_TIMEOUT_MS=1000`, run against a long round; verify `taskkill` on Windows and SIGKILL elsewhere.
- Retry jitter: simulate transient failures; confirm spaced retries and JSONL `retry` events.
- Context budget: place a large `context.txt`; confirm truncation banners and stable latency.
- Rendering: craft outputs with nested code fences and long messages; verify preview fences and “Jump to” anchors.
- Flush on exit: send SIGINT during a write; ensure tail of `.md`/`.jsonl` is present.

**Evaluating logging methods**

Previously, only text was logged without fenced code, which is acceptable, but using logFence for full messages seems safer to prevent nested blocks from causing issues. In a recent commit, there was a change to use logFence on the head but keep full plain to avoid byte duplication. They emphasized ensuring valid markdown for previews, but the full message can still break the document. Using logFence for full does increase overhead, but they aimed for minimal overhead overall.
thinking
**Sanitizing message content**

The initial version of "renderMessage" didn't use fenced blocks, but a newer patch changed the head to be fenced, and now there's a suggestion to also fence the full message. The argument is that fencing the preview prevents issues with half fences, but the unfenced full block could allow HTML conflicts. To be safe, we might need to sanitize content, particularly escaping "</details>" to avoid structure breaks. Wrapping the full message in fenced blocks could be a straightforward solution to prevent HTML injection.

There's also room for improvement in handling boolean values from environment variables. A simple `toBool` helper could clarify parsing, though I'd recommend keeping changes minimal and specific to 'SHELLEY_OUTPUT_CONTRACT'. 

Additionally, the use of content in code fences might overlook syntax highlighting for diff outputs. I'm concerned that wrapping everything in a code fence could affect readability, losing important formatting details.

I see they want to avoid broken Markdown and HTML, which makes sense. A better approach could be to wrap messages in a `<details>` tag and sanitize HTML while allowing code fences to render correctly. If nested backticks are an issue, using four backticks outside could solve that. 

However, wrapping everything in code fences may interfere with rendering and internal formatting. Instead, I propose a function called `renderMessageSafely`, which segments the message to escape only HTML tags while preserving internal Markdown structures. This could provide a safer, cleaner output.

+function toBool(v?: string, def = false) {
+  if (v == null) return def;
+  switch (v.trim().toLowerCase()) {
+    case "1": case "true": case "yes": case "on": return true;
+    case "0": case "false": case "no": case "off": return false;

+}
+
+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");
+}
```

 function log(line: string) {

 function logComment(msg: string) {

 async function runCli(label: string, args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
   const start = Date.now();
   const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
   childProcs.add(proc);
   let timedOut = false;
   const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
   const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
   const killTimer = setTimeout(() => {
     timedOut = true;
     try { proc.kill(); } catch {}
     // escalate if still alive
     setTimeout(() => { try { proc.kill("SIGKILL"); } catch {} }, SIGKILL_AFTER_MS);
   }, TIMEOUT_MS);
   try {
     const code = await proc.exited;
     const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
     const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
     if (timedOut) throw new Error(`timeout after ${TIMEOUT_MS}ms`);
     return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
   } finally {
     clearTimeout(killTimer);
     childProcs.delete(proc);
   }
 }

 function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
   const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
   const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
   const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));

   const inA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensIn");
   const outA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensOut");
   const inB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensIn");
   const outB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensOut");
+  const inT = inA + inB;
+  const outT = outA + outB;

- Reliable subprocesses: kill-on-timeout with SIGKILL escalation; jittered exponential backoff; retries logged; optional stderr blocks.
- Safer JSON parsing: tolerate fenced code blocks or wrappers; fall back to plain text.
- Context guardrails: byte budgets overall/per-file to keep prompts fast and relevant.
- Typesetting: front‑matter, anchors, nav line, collapsible messages (with optional truncation), readable stats table with token totals.
- Unified logging: single write stream + helpers; optional `.jsonl` event stream (off by default).
- Env hygiene: broader provider key stripping (opt-in) to enforce subscription-only runs for spawned CLIs.

**Patch**
Apply this single, self-contained patch to shelley.ts (no new deps).

```diff
diff --git a/shelley.ts b/shelley.ts

+++ b/shelley.ts

+// === Runtime config (env overridable) ===
+const TIMEOUT_MS = Math.max(1, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_TIMEOUT_MS ?? "420000", 10)); // 7m default
+const MAX_RETRIES = Math.max(0, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_RETRIES ?? "1", 10));        // retry once
+const USE_CLAUDE_JSON = (process.env.SHELLEY_CLAUDE_JSON ?? "1") === "1";                 // Claude JSON if possible
+const SIGKILL_AFTER_MS = Math.max(0, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_SIGKILL_AFTER_MS ?? "5000", 10));
+const BACKOFF_BASE_MS  = Math.max(100, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_BACKOFF_BASE_MS  ?? "1500", 10));
+const BACKOFF_MAX_MS   = Math.max(BACKOFF_BASE_MS, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_BACKOFF_MAX_MS ?? "20000", 10));
+const BACKOFF_JITTER   = (process.env.SHELLEY_BACKOFF_JITTER ?? "1") === "1";
+const MAX_CONTEXT_BYTES = Math.max(0, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_MAX_CONTEXT_BYTES ?? "262144", 10));      // 256 KiB
+const MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES = Math.max(0, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES ?? "65536", 10)); // 64 KiB
+const TRUNCATE_LINES = Math.max(0, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_TRUNCATE_LINES ?? "0", 10)); // 0 = no truncation
+const SHOW_NAV = (process.env.SHELLEY_SHOW_NAV ?? "1") === "1";
+const SHOW_STDERR_BLOCKS = (process.env.SHELLEY_SHOW_STDERR ?? "0") === "1";
+const WRITE_JSONL = (process.env.SHELLEY_JSONL ?? "0") === "1";
+const STRIP_PROVIDER_ENVS = (process.env.SHELLEY_STRIP_PROVIDER_ENVS ?? "1") === "1";
+const PROVIDER_PREFIXES = ["OPENAI_", "ANTHROPIC_", "OPENROUTER_", "AZURE_OPENAI", "MISTRAL_", "COHERE_", "TOGETHER_", "GEMINI_", "GOOGLE_", "BEDROCK_", "PERPLEXITY_"];

+function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
   const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
   for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
+  if (STRIP_PROVIDER_ENVS) {
+    for (const k of Object.keys(env)) {
+      if (PROVIDER_PREFIXES.some((p) => k.startsWith(p))) delete env[k];
+    }
+  }
   return env;
 }
 
+// === Logging helpers ===
+function log(line: string) {
+  const s = line + "\n";
+  process.stdout.write(s);
+  if (logStream) logStream.write(s);
+  else appendFileSync(logFile, s);
+}
+function logComment(msg: string) {
+  const safe = msg.replaceAll("-->", "→").replaceAll("--", "—");
+  log(`<!-- ${safe} -->`);
+}
+function logFence(kind: string, body: string) {
+  log("```" + kind);
+  for (const line of body.split("\n")) log(line);
+  log("```");
+}
+function event(type: string, data: Record<string, unknown> = {}) {
+  if (!eventStream) return;
+  const rec = { t: new Date().toISOString(), type, ...data };
+  try { eventStream.write(JSON.stringify(rec) + "\n"); } catch { /* ignore */ }
+}

+  if (!out) throw new Error("claude returned empty output");

+// === Subprocess helpers ===
+async function runCli(label: string, args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
+  const start = Date.now();
+  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
+  childProcs.add(proc);
+  event("cli_start", { label });
+  let timedOut = false;
+  const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
+  const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
+  const killTimer = setTimeout(() => {
+    timedOut = true;
+    try { proc.kill(); } catch {}
+    setTimeout(() => { try { proc.kill("SIGKILL"); } catch {} }, SIGKILL_AFTER_MS);
+  }, TIMEOUT_MS);
+  try {
+    const code = await proc.exited;
+    const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
+    const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
+    if (timedOut) throw new Error(`timeout after ${TIMEOUT_MS}ms`);
+    event("cli_end", { label, code, seconds });
+    return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
+  } finally {
+    clearTimeout(killTimer);
+    childProcs.delete(proc);
+  }
+}
+
+async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
+  let attempt = 0;
+  let lastErr: unknown = null;
+  while (attempt <= MAX_RETRIES) {
+    try { return await fn(); }
+    catch (e) {
+      lastErr = e;
+      if (attempt === MAX_RETRIES) break;
+      const base = Math.min(BACKOFF_MAX_MS, BACKOFF_BASE_MS * Math.pow(2, attempt));
+      const jitter = BACKOFF_JITTER ? Math.floor(Math.random() * base * 0.3) : 0;
+      const backoff = base + jitter;
+      logComment(`retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms`);
+      event("retry", { label, attempt: attempt + 1, backoff_ms: backoff, error: String(e) });
+      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, backoff));
+      attempt += 1;
+    }
+  }
+  throw lastErr instanceof Error ? lastErr : new Error(String(lastErr));
+}
+
+function parseClaudeJson(s: string): { text: string; tokensIn?: number; tokensOut?: number } | null {
+  try {
+    // tolerate wrappers or accidental fences
+    let payload = s.trim();
+    const fence = payload.match(/```json([\s\S]*?)```/i);
+    if (fence) payload = fence[1].trim();
+    else {
+      const first = payload.indexOf("{");
+      const last = payload.lastIndexOf("}");
+      if (first !== -1 && last !== -1) payload = payload.slice(first, last + 1);
+    }
+    const j = JSON.parse(payload);
+    const text =
+      j.text ?? j.output_text ?? j.result ?? j.completion ??
+      (Array.isArray(j.content) ? j.content.map((c: any) => c?.text ?? "").join("\n") : undefined);
+    const tokensIn  = j.token_usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.input_tokens;
+    const tokensOut = j.token_usage?.output_tokens ?? j.usage?.output_tokens ?? j.output_tokens;
+    if (typeof text === "string" && text.trim()) {
+      return {
+        text: text.trim(),
+        tokensIn: Number.isFinite(tokensIn) ? tokensIn : undefined,
+        tokensOut: Number.isFinite(tokensOut) ? tokensOut : undefined
+      };
+    }
+  } catch { /* best-effort */ }
+  return null;
+}
+

 const DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL = process.env.CODEX_MODEL ?? "gpt-5";

 // === Context loading ===
 
 function loadContext(topicFile: string | undefined, repoRoot: string): string {
   if (!topicFile) return "";
   const listPath = resolve(dirname(topicFile), "context.txt");
   if (!existsSync(listPath)) return "";
   let out = "";
+  let budget = MAX_CONTEXT_BYTES;
   for (const rel of readFileSync(listPath, "utf8")
     .split("\n")
     .map((l) => l.trim())
     .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#"))) {
     const abs = resolve(repoRoot, rel);
     if (!existsSync(abs)) {
       console.error(`Context file not found: ${rel}`);
       process.exit(1);
     }
-    out += `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${readFileSync(abs, "utf8")}`;
+    if (budget <= 0) break;
+    let text = readFileSync(abs, "utf8");
+    if (text.length > MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES) text = text.slice(0, MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES) + "\n… [truncated]";
+    const block = `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${text}`;
+    const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(block).length;
+    if (bytes <= budget) {
+      out += block;
+      budget -= bytes;
+    } else {
+      const slice = Math.max(0, budget - 32);
+      const cut = block.slice(0, slice) + "\n… [context budget exhausted]";
+      out += cut;
+      budget = 0;
+      break;
+    }
   }
   return out;
 }

 // === Stats footer ===
 
 function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
   const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
   const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
   const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));
+  const sumTok = (rows: TurnRecord[], k: "tokensIn"|"tokensOut") => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + (t[k] ?? 0), 0);
+  const inA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensIn");
+  const outA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensOut");
+  const inB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensIn");
+  const outB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensOut");
+  const inT = inA + inB;
+  const outT = outA + outB;

+// === Rendering helpers ===
+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
+    log(""); log(text); log(""); log("</details>");
+    return;
+  }
+  const lines = text.split("\n");
+  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  const tail = lines.slice(TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
+  log(""); log(head); log(""); log("</details>");
+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(tail); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+function navLine(rounds: number): string {
+  const cells: string[] = [];
+  for (let r = 1; r <= rounds; r++) cells.push(`[${r}A](#round-${r}-a)·[${r}B](#round-${r}-b)`);
+  return cells.join("  |  ");
+}

+    if (logStream) { try { logStream.end(); } catch {} }

**Prompt/UX Tweaks**
- Add a strict output contract to both agents to improve readability: “Respond with exactly three sections: Summary (≤3 bullets), Patch (unified diff in a fenced diff block), Notes (≤5 bullets). For reviewer, add OPEN QUESTIONS if any.” Keep “Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.”

**Why this helps**
- Reliability: real timeouts kill children, retries are backoff+jittered, and stderr is visible when needed. Signals and failures are captured and logged.
- Architecture: subprocess, logging, parsing, rendering isolated as helpers inside the same file; easier to test/extend without adding deps.
- Readability: front‑matter for indexing, quick nav, collapsible/truncated messages, and token telemetry make long debates skimmable and analyzable.
- Analytics/resume: optional `.jsonl` gives one-line events for turns, retries, stderr, and lifecycle without affecting markdown.

**Optional Next Steps**
- Add `SHELLEY_ON_FAIL=skip|abort|noop` to let runs continue when a turn exhausts retries.
- Emit a `.md.index.json` with per-round offsets to jump in viewers.
- Small CLI polish (no deps): accept `--rounds N`, `--topic "..."`, `--topic-file path`, `--log-dir path` in addition to current positional flags.

**Tradeoffs**
- Truncated preview as a fenced `text` block duplicates some bytes, but guarantees valid Markdown when agent output contains its own fences.
- Byte-capping Codex prompts may drop the oldest turns earlier than the fixed window; safer than risking CLI rejections for oversize inputs.

**Open Questions**
- On failure policy: do you want `SHELLEY_ON_FAIL=abort|skip` to continue a debate when one agent exhausts retries?
- Do we cap child stdout/stderr size (e.g., `SHELLEY_MAX_CHARS`) to prevent runaway logs, or prefer full fidelity?
- Should JSONL include raw prompts/responses for audit (privacy vs. analytics)?

**Test Plan**
- Timeout path: set `SHELLEY_TIMEOUT_MS=1000`, run against a long round; verify `taskkill` on Windows and SIGKILL elsewhere.
- Retry jitter: simulate transient failures; confirm spaced retries and JSONL `retry` events.
- Context budget: place a large `context.txt`; confirm truncation banners and stable latency.
- Rendering: craft outputs with nested code fences and long messages; verify preview fences and “Jump to” anchors.
- Flush on exit: send SIGINT during a write; ensure tail of `.md`/`.jsonl` is present.

-const PROVIDER_PREFIXES = ["OPENAI_", "ANTHROPIC_", "OPENROUTER_", "AZURE_OPENAI", "MISTRAL_", "COHERE_", "TOGETHER_", "GEMINI_", "GOOGLE_", "BEDROCK_", "PERPLEXITY_"];

+const INCLUDE_OUTPUT_CONTRACT = toBool(process.env.SHELLEY_OUTPUT_CONTRACT, false);
+
+function toBool(v?: string, def = false) {
+  if (v == null) return def;
+  switch (v.trim().toLowerCase()) {
+    case "1": case "true": case "yes": case "on": return true;
+    case "0": case "false": case "no": case "off": return false;
+    default: return def;
+  }
+}
@@
-function renderMessage(text: string) {
-  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
-    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
-    log(""); logFence("text", text); log("</details>");
-    return;
-  }
-  const lines = text.split("\n");
-  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
-  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
-  log(""); logFence("text", head); log("</details>");
-  log("");
-  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
-  log(""); logFence("text", text); log("</details>");
-}
+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  const out = escapeHtmlOutsideFences(text);
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
+    log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+    return;
+  }
+  const lines = text.split("\n");
+  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
+  log(""); logFence("text", head); log("</details>");
+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+
+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");
+}
```

Notes
- Outer code-fencing the whole message prevents inner ```diff blocks from rendering; escape HTML outside fences instead to preserve formatting and avoid tag injection.
- Defaulting `SHELLEY_OUTPUT_CONTRACT` to on is a behavioral change; switch to opt‑in for backward compatibility (flip default in a minor release if desired).
- Added `AZURE_OPENAI_` to `PROVIDER_PREFIXES` so stripping catches both forms.
- Consider reasserting a short “remember the contract” prefix on resumed turns in case some backends drop system prompts.
- If `logFence` doesn’t pick longer fences when content contains ``` sequences, add a smart variant to avoid fence collisions.

OPEN QUESTIONS
- Does `resume` reliably persist prior system prompts across all configured providers?
- Do you want contract-on-by-default guarded by a version bump or a release note?
- Should we add a lightweight validator to warn when outputs violate the contract?

+  const fence = "`".repeat(Math.max(3, maxTicks + 1));

+
+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");
+}

+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");

 function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
   const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };

 function log(line: string) {
   const s = line + "\n";
   process.stdout.write(s);
   if (logStream) logStream.write(s);
   else appendFileSync(logFile, s);

 function logComment(msg: string) {
   const safe = msg.replaceAll("-->", "→").replaceAll("--", "—");
   log(`<!-- ${safe} -->`);

+function logFence(kind: string, body: string) {
+  log("```" + kind);
+  for (const line of body.split("\n")) log(line);
+  log("```");
+}
@@
 async function runCli(label: string, args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
   const start = Date.now();
   const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
   childProcs.add(proc);
   let timedOut = false;
   const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
   const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
   const killTimer = setTimeout(() => {
     timedOut = true;
     try { proc.kill(); } catch {}
     // escalate if still alive
     setTimeout(() => { try { proc.kill("SIGKILL"); } catch {} }, SIGKILL_AFTER_MS);
   }, TIMEOUT_MS);
   try {
     const code = await proc.exited;
     const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
     const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
     if (timedOut) throw new Error(`timeout after ${TIMEOUT_MS}ms`);
     return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
   } finally {
     clearTimeout(killTimer);
     childProcs.delete(proc);
   }
 }

+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");

+  log(""); log(head); log(""); log("</details>");
+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(tail); log(""); log("</details>");

 function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
   const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
   const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
   const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));
   const sumTok = (rows: TurnRecord[], k: "tokensIn"|"tokensOut") => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + (t[k] ?? 0), 0);
   const inA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensIn");
   const outA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensOut");
   const inB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensIn");
   const outB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensOut");

**Notes**
- Transcript readability: truncation keeps logs scannable while preserving full text behind details; the “Jump to” nav speeds cross-round comparisons.
- Reliability: stderr blocks are opt-in to avoid noise but invaluable for flaky runs; unified logging avoids partial writes.
- JSON parsing now tolerates accidental fenced output if a CLI wraps JSON; still falls back to plain text if parsing fails.
- Consider adding a tiny `.jsonl` event stream next (turn_start/turn_end/retry/stderr/signal) to enable resume and analytics; keep it off by default via `SHELLEY_JSONL=0`.

Current user message:
[Creativity: 3/5] Mix new ideas with refinement. Address open questions. Weigh tradeoffs.

**Summary**
- Keep the CLI-subscription path and make it resilient: timeouts that actually terminate children, jittered backoff + retries, stronger signal handling, bounded context, and optional JSONL event log for analytics/resume.
- Improve architecture in-place (no new deps): unify logging, subprocess, and parsing helpers; add small rendering helpers; keep single-file but with clearer sections.
- Upgrade transcript readability: front‑matter, anchors + “Jump to” nav, collapsible messages with optional truncation, token telemetry in per‑round rows and totals, optional collapsed stderr blocks.

**Key Improvements**
- Reliable subprocesses: kill-on-timeout with SIGKILL escalation; jittered exponential backoff; retries logged; optional stderr blocks.
- Safer JSON parsing: tolerate fenced code blocks or wrappers; fall back to plain text.
- Context guardrails: byte budgets overall/per-file to keep prompts fast and relevant.
- Typesetting: front‑matter, anchors, nav line, collapsible messages (with optional truncation), readable stats table with token totals.
- Unified logging: single write stream + helpers; optional `.jsonl` event stream (off by default).
- Env hygiene: broader provider key stripping (opt-in) to enforce subscription-only runs for spawned CLIs.

**Patch**
Apply this single, self-contained patch to shelley.ts (no new deps).

+function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {

+// === Subprocess helpers ===
+async function runCli(label: string, args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
+  const start = Date.now();
+  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
+  childProcs.add(proc);
+  event("cli_start", { label });
+  let timedOut = false;
+  const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
+  const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
+  const killTimer = setTimeout(() => {
+    timedOut = true;
+    try { proc.kill(); } catch {}
+    setTimeout(() => { try { proc.kill("SIGKILL"); } catch {} }, SIGKILL_AFTER_MS);
+  }, TIMEOUT_MS);
+  try {
+    const code = await proc.exited;
+    const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
+    const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
+    if (timedOut) throw new Error(`timeout after ${TIMEOUT_MS}ms`);
+    event("cli_end", { label, code, seconds });
+    return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
+  } finally {
+    clearTimeout(killTimer);
+    childProcs.delete(proc);
+  }
+}
+
+async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
+  let attempt = 0;
+  let lastErr: unknown = null;
+  while (attempt <= MAX_RETRIES) {
+    try { return await fn(); }
+    catch (e) {
+      lastErr = e;
+      if (attempt === MAX_RETRIES) break;
+      const base = Math.min(BACKOFF_MAX_MS, BACKOFF_BASE_MS * Math.pow(2, attempt));
+      const jitter = BACKOFF_JITTER ? Math.floor(Math.random() * base * 0.3) : 0;
+      const backoff = base + jitter;
+      logComment(`retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms`);
+      event("retry", { label, attempt: attempt + 1, backoff_ms: backoff, error: String(e) });
+      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, backoff));
+      attempt += 1;
+    }
+  }
+  throw lastErr instanceof Error ? lastErr : new Error(String(lastErr));
+}
+
+function parseClaudeJson(s: string): { text: string; tokensIn?: number; tokensOut?: number } | null {
+  try {
+    // tolerate wrappers or accidental fences
+    let payload = s.trim();
+    const fence = payload.match(/```json([\s\S]*?)```/i);
+    if (fence) payload = fence[1].trim();
+    else {
+      const first = payload.indexOf("{");
+      const last = payload.lastIndexOf("}");
+      if (first !== -1 && last !== -1) payload = payload.slice(first, last + 1);
+    }
+    const j = JSON.parse(payload);
+    const text =
+      j.text ?? j.output_text ?? j.result ?? j.completion ??
+      (Array.isArray(j.content) ? j.content.map((c: any) => c?.text ?? "").join("\n") : undefined);
+    const tokensIn  = j.token_usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.input_tokens;
+    const tokensOut = j.token_usage?.output_tokens ?? j.usage?.output_tokens ?? j.output_tokens;
+    if (typeof text === "string" && text.trim()) {
+      return {
+        text: text.trim(),
+        tokensIn: Number.isFinite(tokensIn) ? tokensIn : undefined,
+        tokensOut: Number.isFinite(tokensOut) ? tokensOut : undefined
+      };
+    }
+  } catch { /* best-effort */ }
+  return null;
+}
+
 // === Codex backend ===

 // === Context loading ===
 
 function loadContext(topicFile: string | undefined, repoRoot: string): string {
   if (!topicFile) return "";
   const listPath = resolve(dirname(topicFile), "context.txt");
   if (!existsSync(listPath)) return "";
   let out = "";
+  let budget = MAX_CONTEXT_BYTES;
   for (const rel of readFileSync(listPath, "utf8")
     .split("\n")
     .map((l) => l.trim())
     .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#"))) {
     const abs = resolve(repoRoot, rel);
     if (!existsSync(abs)) {
       console.error(`Context file not found: ${rel}`);
       process.exit(1);
     }
-    out += `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${readFileSync(abs, "utf8")}`;
+    if (budget <= 0) break;
+    let text = readFileSync(abs, "utf8");
+    if (text.length > MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES) text = text.slice(0, MAX_CONTEXT_FILE_BYTES) + "\n… [truncated]";
+    const block = `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${text}`;
+    const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(block).length;
+    if (bytes <= budget) {
+      out += block;
+      budget -= bytes;
+    } else {
+      const slice = Math.max(0, budget - 32);
+      const cut = block.slice(0, slice) + "\n… [context budget exhausted]";
+      out += cut;
+      budget = 0;
+      break;
+    }
   }
   return out;
 }

 // === Stats footer ===
 
 function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
   const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
   const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
   const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));
+  const sumTok = (rows: TurnRecord[], k: "tokensIn"|"tokensOut") => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + (t[k] ?? 0), 0);
+  const inA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensIn");
+  const outA = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="A"), "tokensOut");
+  const inB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensIn");
+  const outB = sumTok(turns.filter((t)=>t.agent==="B"), "tokensOut");
+  const inT = inA + inB;
+  const outT = outA + outB;
 
   log("<details><summary><strong>Stats</strong></summary>");
   log("");
-  log("| Round | Agent | Duration |");
-  log("|------:|:-----:|---------:|");
+  log("| Round | Agent | Duration | Tokens (in/out) |");

+    log(`| ${t.round} | ${t.agent} | ${t.seconds}s | ${tok} |`);

-  log(`| | **Agent A** | **${sA}s** |`);
-  log(`| | **Agent B** | **${sB}s** |`);

+  log(`| | **Agent B** | **${sB}s** | ${inB || outB ? `${inB}/${outB}` : "—"} |`);
+  log(`| | **Total** | **${sA + sB}s** | ${inT || outT ? `${inT}/${outT}` : "—"} |`);

 }
 
+// === Rendering helpers ===
+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
+    log(""); log(text); log(""); log("</details>");
+    return;
+  }
+  const lines = text.split("\n");
+  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  const tail = lines.slice(TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
+  log(""); log(head); log(""); log("</details>");
+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(tail); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+function navLine(rounds: number): string {
+  const cells: string[] = [];
+  for (let r = 1; r <= rounds; r++) cells.push(`[${r}A](#round-${r}-a)·[${r}B](#round-${r}-b)`);
+  return cells.join("  |  ");
+}

**Prompt/UX Tweaks**
- Add a strict output contract to both agents to improve readability: “Respond with exactly three sections: Summary (≤3 bullets), Patch (unified diff in a fenced diff block), Notes (≤5 bullets). For reviewer, add OPEN QUESTIONS if any.” Keep “Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.”

**Why this helps**
- Reliability: real timeouts kill children, retries are backoff+jittered, and stderr is visible when needed. Signals and failures are captured and logged.
- Architecture: subprocess, logging, parsing, rendering isolated as helpers inside the same file; easier to test/extend without adding deps.
- Readability: front‑matter for indexing, quick nav, collapsible/truncated messages, and token telemetry make long debates skimmable and analyzable.
- Analytics/resume: optional `.jsonl` gives one-line events for turns, retries, stderr, and lifecycle without affecting markdown.

**Optional Next Steps**
- Add `SHELLEY_ON_FAIL=skip|abort|noop` to let runs continue when a turn exhausts retries.
- Emit a `.md.index.json` with per-round offsets to jump in viewers.
- Small CLI polish (no deps): accept `--rounds N`, `--topic "..."`, `--topic-file path`, `--log-dir path` in addition to current positional flags.

**Verdict**
Your patch is strong. It hardens subprocess handling, bounds context, improves typesetting, and adds optional JSONL telemetry without breaking the subscription-only CLI workflow. Below are five micro-fixes to tighten edge cases and polish UX.

**Targeted Micro‑Patches**
- Move anchors before headings for reliable “Jump to” behavior.
- Make truncated previews fence-safe and show the full message in the closed block.
- Cap Codex prompt size by bytes in addition to turn-window count.
- Add Windows escalation fallback via `taskkill` when SIGKILL is unavailable.
- Flush log/event streams before exiting to avoid dropped tail writes.

+    Promise.all([endStream(logStream), endStream(eventStream)]).then(() => {
+      process.stdout.write(`\nLog saved to ${logFile}\n`);
+      process.exit(code);
+    });
+  }
```

**Tradeoffs**
- Truncated preview as a fenced `text` block duplicates some bytes, but guarantees valid Markdown when agent output contains its own fences.
- Byte-capping Codex prompts may drop the oldest turns earlier than the fixed window; safer than risking CLI rejections for oversize inputs.

**Open Questions**
- On failure policy: do you want `SHELLEY_ON_FAIL=abort|skip` to continue a debate when one agent exhausts retries?
- Do we cap child stdout/stderr size (e.g., `SHELLEY_MAX_CHARS`) to prevent runaway logs, or prefer full fidelity?
- Should JSONL include raw prompts/responses for audit (privacy vs. analytics)?

**Test Plan**
- Timeout path: set `SHELLEY_TIMEOUT_MS=1000`, run against a long round; verify `taskkill` on Windows and SIGKILL elsewhere.
- Retry jitter: simulate transient failures; confirm spaced retries and JSONL `retry` events.
- Context budget: place a large `context.txt`; confirm truncation banners and stable latency.
- Rendering: craft outputs with nested code fences and long messages; verify preview fences and “Jump to” anchors.
- Flush on exit: send SIGINT during a write; ensure tail of `.md`/`.jsonl` is present.
tokens used
32 743 -->

-const PROVIDER_PREFIXES = ["OPENAI_", "ANTHROPIC_", "OPENROUTER_", "AZURE_OPENAI", "MISTRAL_", "COHERE_", "TOGETHER_", "GEMINI_", "GOOGLE_", "BEDROCK_", "PERPLEXITY_"];

+const INCLUDE_OUTPUT_CONTRACT = toBool(process.env.SHELLEY_OUTPUT_CONTRACT, false);
+
+function toBool(v?: string, def = false) {
+  if (v == null) return def;
+  switch (v.trim().toLowerCase()) {
+    case "1": case "true": case "yes": case "on": return true;
+    case "0": case "false": case "no": case "off": return false;
+    default: return def;
+  }
+}
@@
-function renderMessage(text: string) {
-  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
-    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
-    log(""); logFence("text", text); log("</details>");
-    return;
-  }
-  const lines = text.split("\n");
-  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
-  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
-  log(""); logFence("text", head); log("</details>");
-  log("");
-  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
-  log(""); logFence("text", text); log("</details>");
-}
+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  const out = escapeHtmlOutsideFences(text);
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
+    log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+    return;
+  }
+  const lines = text.split("\n");
+  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");

+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+
+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");
+}
```

Notes
- Outer code-fencing the whole message prevents inner ```diff blocks from rendering; escape HTML outside fences instead to preserve formatting and avoid tag injection.
- Defaulting `SHELLEY_OUTPUT_CONTRACT` to on is a behavioral change; switch to opt‑in for backward compatibility (flip default in a minor release if desired).
- Added `AZURE_OPENAI_` to `PROVIDER_PREFIXES` so stripping catches both forms.
- Consider reasserting a short “remember the contract” prefix on resumed turns in case some backends drop system prompts.
- If `logFence` doesn’t pick longer fences when content contains ``` sequences, add a smart variant to avoid fence collisions.

OPEN QUESTIONS
- Does `resume` reliably persist prior system prompts across all configured providers?
- Do you want contract-on-by-default guarded by a version bump or a release note?
- Should we add a lightweight validator to warn when outputs violate the contract?

The escapeHtmlOutsideFences logically toggles lines with "```," but we must ensure it accurately checks only for lines that start with exactly three backticks. If quadruple ticks appear, that toggling won't be detected, but it's rare. The adjustments we made to logFence should help here as well.

+function toBool(v?: string, def = false) {
+  if (v == null) return def;
+  switch (v.trim().toLowerCase()) {
+    case "1": case "true": case "yes": case "on": return true;

+  const fence = "`".repeat(Math.max(3, maxTicks + 1));

+  log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+
+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");
+}

+  if (v == null) return def;
+  switch (v.trim().toLowerCase()) {
+    case "1": case "true": case "yes": case "on": return true;
+    case "0": case "false": case "no": case "off": return false;

+function logFence(kind: string, body: string) {
+  const runs = body.match(/`+/g);
+  const maxTicks = runs ? Math.max(0, ...runs.map(s => s.length)) : 0;
+  const fence = "`".repeat(Math.max(3, maxTicks + 1));
+  log(fence + (kind ? kind : ""));
+  for (const line of body.split("\n")) log(line);

+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+
+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");
+}

They use "trimStart()" to determine the 't' variable and check if "t.startsWith('```')", which ignores indentation — that really makes sense since many code fences start at column 0. 

Next, they toggle "inFence" based on the line with '```', which works well. Now for the "renderMessage" truncated path, it splits the text by new lines for length measurement. Even though they compute 'head' to reference the first TRUNCATE_LINES lines, they still use 'head' unescaped when calling 'logFence("text", head)'. +function toBool(v?: string, def = false) {
+  if (v == null) return def;
+  switch (v.trim().toLowerCase()) {
+    case "1": case "true": case "yes": case "on": return true;
+    case "0": case "false": case "no": case "off": return false;
+    default: return def;

-function logFence(kind: string, body: string) {
-  log("```" + kind);
-  for (const line of body.split("\n")) log(line);
-  log("```");
-}
+function logFence(kind: string, body: string) {
+  const runs = body.match(/`+/g);
+  const maxTicks = runs ? Math.max(0, ...runs.map(s => s.length)) : 0;
+  const fence = "`".repeat(Math.max(3, maxTicks + 1));
+  log(fence + (kind ? kind : ""));
+  for (const line of body.split("\n")) log(line);
+  log(fence);
+}

+function renderMessage(text: string) {
+  const out = escapeHtmlOutsideFences(text);
+  if (!TRUNCATE_LINES || text.split("\n").length <= TRUNCATE_LINES) {
+    log("<details open><summary>Message</summary>");
+    log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+    return;
+  }
+  const lines = text.split("\n");
+  const head = lines.slice(0, TRUNCATE_LINES).join("\n");
+  log("<details open><summary>Message (truncated)</summary>");
+  log(""); logFence("text", head); log("</details>");
+  log("");
+  log(`<details><summary>Show full message (+${lines.length - TRUNCATE_LINES} lines)</summary>`);
+  log(""); log(out); log(""); log("</details>");
+}
+
+function escapeHtmlOutsideFences(input: string): string {
+  let inFence = false;
+  return input.split("\n").map(line => {
+    const t = line.trimStart();
+    if (t.startsWith("```")) { inFence = !inFence; return line; }
+    return inFence ? line : line.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
+  }).join("\n");
+}
